Exit Site
If you are in danger, call 911. If you need to exit this website quickly, click on the ESCAPE button. This button will immediately open a browser window for weather.com and replace your current window with google.com.

## The .gov means it's official. 
Local, state, and federal government websites often end in .gov. Commonwealth of Pennsylvania government websites and email systems use "pennsylvania.gov" or "pa.gov" at the end of the address. Before sharing sensitive or personal information, make sure you're on an official state website.

# Death Statistics
These PDF reports contain various tables of death statistics organized by levels of geography available and the primary topic for each report. Click "Show +" to see a group of reports, and "Hide -" to collapse the list down. To open a specific report, select the desired year and click the "Submit" button next to the report.  

View detailed [2020-2023 COVID-19 death statistics(opens in a new tab)](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/covid.html).
**Disclaimer:** If you use any of the data provided, please include the following statement in any publication or release: "These data were provided by the Pennsylvania Department of Health. The Department specifically disclaims responsibility for any analyses, interpretations, or conclusions."
###  List of State Statistics
Most recent data:
  * [Deaths by Age, Sex, Race, and Year; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeSexRaceYear_PA_2019_2023.pdf)
  * [Deaths by Selected Causes, Age, Race, Sex, and Hispanic Origin; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeSexRaceHispanicCause_PA_2023.pdf)
  * [Deaths by Age, Sex, Race, and ICD-10 Code (A00-Y98); Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeSexRaceICD_PA_2023.pdf)
  * [Deaths by Age, Sex, Race, and ICD-9 Code (001-999); State Total, Pennsylvania](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeSexRaceICD_PA_1998.pdf)  

  * [Deaths by Selected Causes, Age, Race, and Sex; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeSexRaceCause_PA_2019_2023.pdf)
  * [Deaths by Selected Causes, Age, Hispanic Origin, and Year; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeHispYearCause_PA_2019_2023.pdf)
  * [Deaths by Selected Causes, Age; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_AgeIndicatorsCause_PA_2019_2023.pdf)
  * [Infant Deaths by Age, Sex, Race, and Year; Pennsylvania Residents](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/Death_InfantAgeSexRaceYear_PA_2019_2023.pdf)

###  Preliminary Statistics
### Preliminary 2024 data  

The [Preliminary Pennsylvania occurrence death data](https://www.pa.gov/content/dam/copapwp-pagov/en/health/documents/topics/healthstatistics/vitalstatistics/deathstatistics/documents/death-preliminary-occurrence-2024.zip) (ZIP) contains death counts by:
  * Year of death
  * Month of death
  * County of occurrence
  * Manner of death

Commonwealth of PennsylvaniaDepartment of Health Page 2 Division of Health Informatics Resident Infant Deaths for Those of Hispanic Origin by Age, Sex, Race and Year State Total, Pennsylvania, 2019-2023 (Unknowns Included in Total) See Last Page for Important Note on Race Total Race and Sex Deaths < 28 Days 28-364 Days State Total WM 101 73 28 WF 87 62 25 BM 18 6 12 BF 19 12 7 OM 151 94 57 OF 125 82 43 Total 518 342 176 WM=White Male WF=White Female BM=Black Male BF=Black Female OM=Male of All Other Races OF=Female of All Other Races Notes: Starting in 2013, race of decedent was derived from multiple race selections. Prior to 2013, race of decedent was derived from a single race designation. For example, starting in 2013, 'White' means that it was the only race selected from a list of multiple race selections. Prior to 2013, 'White' means that the single race designation was 'White'. Also, starting in 2013, 'All Other Races' includes 'Multi-Race' (more than one race selected).
